< text>
While the office was not the cleanest, the hygienist was very kind, and I was able to get a cleaning with no issue.
However, anyone who is looking to get wisdom teeth extracted here should be very cautious. I was told, by the secretary, that the oral surgeon will not extract wisdom teeth without doing bone grafting, which costs around $1800 out of pocket, since it is cosmetic and not covered. Everyone should do their own research, but this is uncommon for many wisdom teeth extractions. I was able to get the opinion of an outside oral specialist who advised me against doing this procedure. It seems like this is a scam some offices will try to pull when they want more than the insurance payout. If they refuse to extract your wisdom teeth without a bone graft, definitely get a second professional opinion and don't get taken advantage of.< /text>

< Review>
From their customer service being phenomenal before I ever even placed an order, to the quality and care exhibited with my delivery, to the volume and variety of succulents I received (more than I even ordered), I cannot possibly praise The Succulent Source enough. < userid>
110458677109097440518</userid>
<pictures>None</pictures>< Review>
It's a small place, but a cozy spot. A lot of other places nearby like the Steel Craft district - grab a drink, feel like a pizza, head on over to PowWow Pizza Co.

My wife and I had the Angkor and the Korean pizzas. Thr flavors on both were very delicious and very unique in their own right. The Angkor had lemon-grass beef on it, which isn't traditionally on pizza, yet the flavor combination was FANTASTIC! The Korean pizza boasted a bulgogi beef and was built on a scientific recipe for my specific taste buds. They have your traditional pizzas as well, cooking away in the fire oven, but why wouldn't you want to try something different? Something like a roasted duck pizza? Which is on my list next after I work off this small pizza I devoured on my own.

The prices are very reasonable, $7 for a small pizza and I even caught a beer (Angkor) for about $5. They also are a part of delivery services, so if you're looking to stay in, they got you covered. Friendly staff and fast service. Give it a shot!<//Review>

< Review>
We starting going here for the Crying Tiger dish. This was the only Thai Food location that we could find that offered the dish. We've discovered that almost every dish is exceptional over our 2 dozen + trips. On our most recent visit we tried the Pad Thai and my wife agreed it was the best we've had. It was well balanced without an over bearing amount of peanuts or peanut sauce as many locations are prone to doing.

Each of their curry dishes are consistently good and their massaman curry is very good.

If highly recommend a visit if you are in the area.</Review>

Rainier Apolonio<//user_name>

1530900601302< /Time>
< rating>
5<//rating>
< text>
TL;DR Version
- Amazing and friendly staff
- Workout equipment is all new (as of 5/9/18)
- Private showers and towel service provided
- Mature crowd and intimate, boutique experience
- Fair pricing with included amenities and services

This is by far the best gym experience I've had compared to many other established gyms such as 24 Hour and LA Fitness. I've been going here for a couple of months now and have always had the same consistent and positive experience since I've signed on as a member.

The staff is very friendly, greeting me every time I visit. They are always willing to help and try to get to know all of their usual gym comers. I received a free fitness consultation on my first day and a 30 day workout plan to get my fitness routine going. It's been several months and the staff still check up on me to see how I am progressing with my fitness journey. Kudos to the team for creating such a positive environment.

I've been coming to this gym pretty consistently since I've started and its nice to see that there is available parking no matter what time I go during the day. They have a private lot, which sometimes gets full, but not to a point where you cannot accommodate yourself to find a spot near the facility.

Compared to other Anytime Fitness gym facilities, this is definitely on the newer side. I would even consider it one of their flagship facilities. They have plenty of amenities such as towel service, private room showers, free Wi-Fi (the good kind), and a workout studio featuring virtual classroom sessions projected onto a wall. The equipment is all new; there are even some equipment in this location that I do not find at other Anytime Fitness facilities. Other features include a heart rate monitoring system that is broadcasted onto dedicated TVs to help you get a strenuous workout.

The gym itself is on the smaller side in comparison to other established gyms such as 24 Hour and LA Fitness. However, that has not really affected my experience at the gym. I actually like the smaller boutique feel, giving it a more intimate experience. Pricing is on the higher side (as of this writing, I currently pay $45/month with an annual renewal), but the price is justified with all the amenities and services I receive from the gym. Members must be 18 or older, allowing for a more mature crowd that will keep equipment racked and the facilities clean.

The gym is staffed during the weekday (9AM-7PM as of this writing). Saturday's, the staff leaves early at 3PM; Sunday's are not staffed at all. If you plan to workout when it is not staffed, I recommend bringing in your own sweat towel. The clean leftover towels provided during unstaffed hours tend to get used quickly. Gym members can enter anytime using the key fob they received upon sign up. I've visited the gym during the early hours of the morning and have had no issues entering/exiting the facility.

Overall, I highly recommend this gym to anyone looking for a more boutique, personalized experience with fair pricing and amazing staff. It's always been a pleasure working out at this location and is considered my home gym for the foreseeable future. Kudos again to the Anytime Fitness team for creating such an amazing environment for all to enjoy.<//text>

<Text>I had to get a contrast ct abdominal/pelvic scan. My insurance required precertification. One local hospital took far too many days to process it and then only got partial approval because they separated the precert as two procedures.

Another hospital would do the scan without precert but was charging me $2000 up front as out of network and I would be responsible for whatever the insurance wouldn't cover!!!

Total at Simon Med would be less than $1900 if my insurance doesn't pay. Simon has the best prices nearby. My only strike is that it would be better if they had a precertification department that customers could contact. They are in my ppo network so I'm hopeful that my insurance takes care of the bill.

<Rating>5</Rating><Text>Very good experience, highly recommend!!

- before I went, I checked the reviews and find out the main problem is deal with payment. So I well prepared before I went. I called on last Wed and got an appointment Friday(yesterday). I received my approval letter from my insurance company and brought it with me. Receptionist don't need it and just asked for my ID and ins card.
- Receptionist are very nice and helpful :
The receptionist(forgot to ask her name) was nice and explained to me when I had questions from the forms, when I finished the first page, she took it and process first so I was called not even I finished completing all forms.
I want to get a copy of my MRI and I forgot to mention yesterday when I left so I went back this morning and I was lucky that they are open. Although their office shows closed on Saturday but they open for patients with appointment. Receptionist Cindy was very nice to burn the CD right away for me.
- Technican Mike was very nice and gentle. He    answered any questions that I asked. Now I know the difference between a normal MRI and an open MRI. If people don't feel comfortable to get into a closed MRI, they can choose the open one but it will be at least double the time. My coworker told me that  his whole MRI appointment took nearly 1-1/2 to 2hrs but it only took me 40mins. 1.5T might be 10-15 mins longer than 3T machine depend on what part of the body so 3T is the fastest, heehee...
- very convenience to change to another location. This company is a group, I make a simple call and changed my appointment from San Francisco to Daly City and I don't need to give my insurance info again.
- feel comfortable, although they don't have music to listen but with double ear plugs, put into my ears and add a headset ear plug outside, it cuts down a lot of noise. Of course you can still hear it, but I just treated it as different types of music rymthum. With the blanklet totally cover me, it makes me feel very comfortable and relax, so time go fast.
- very easy parking, they are located at the same building of AAA with a huge free parking lot.

Thanks SimonMed Imaging/Daly City!<//Text>< pictures>
